[TELEPORT_AXIOMS_IMPLEMENTED]
H(L) := 16 + 8 * leb_len(8*L)
C_END(bitpos) := 3 + pad_to_byte(bitpos + 3)
C_CAUS(op, params, L) := 3 + 8*leb_len(op) + Σ 8*leb_len(param_i) + 8*leb_len(L)
pad_to_byte(x) := (8 - (x mod 8)) mod 8

leb_len(n) implementation:
  if n == 0: return 1
  length = 0
  while n > 0:
    length += 1
    n >>= 7
  return length
